Dalhousie rakavambwa somunhu nonsectarian kukoreji 1818 nokuda eponymous mutevedzeri wagavhuna pamusoro Nova Scotia, George Ramsay, 9fung Earl pamusoro Dalhousie. The kukoreji haana kunyarara kirasi yacho yokutanga kusvikira 1838, kusvikira ipapo uchishanda apo neapo nokuda nematambudziko emari. It rakavhurwa kechitatu mune 1863 kutevera nokubatanidzwazve kuti akaunza kuchinja zita kuti “Nemagavhuna Dalhousie College uye University”. Yunivhesiti pamutemo achinja zita raro “Dalhousie University” mu 1997 kuburikidza mitemo dzematunhu, chete mitemo zvibatanidzwe kupfungwa pamwe Technical University of Nova Scotia.
